real-life situations.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>How The Gift - Beta uses personal data</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">The personal data collected from The App used to continuously improve your experience by informing feature updates that serve your best interest.&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Additionally, The App may use the Personal Data we collect to:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Process your payment.</p></li><li><p class="" you.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Communicate with you about our App or to inform you of any changes to the same.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Provide data with collaboration partners such as organizations enterprises and our network of current and future partners for product improvement purposes.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p></li></ul><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Data Sharing with Strategic Partners</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Periodically <span style="text-decoration:underline">Tha App</span> may extract an anonymized set of data from <span style="text-decoration:underline">The App’s</span> cloud-based environment. What this means is a small sample of the data stored in the cloud, and then remove all any and all potential personal identifiable information (PII) leaving just the session data in place. This non-identifiable user data set is then used for product improvement purposes in clinical trials, research projects, enterprise or organizational benefit studies and related analysis with the intent of proving efficacy and/or improving the product experience.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>How personal data is collected</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Personal Data that you voluntarily provide through <span style="text-decoration:underline">The App</span> or that is automatically collected through your use of The App. Personal Data is collected through the App these ways:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Active player input during App usage such as email, username, password and more.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Passive data and information during App usage</p></li></ul><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Personal Data We Collect</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We collect the following Personal Data through your use of <span style="text-decoration:underline">The App</span>:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Device ID of your VR headset and associated data available at Device ID data level</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Information provided by you during app usage as relating to activities&nbsp;</p></li></ul><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Categories of Data Collected</strong></p>

  <h4 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Storage &amp; Retention of Personal Data</strong></h4><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">The data collected and used by <span style="text-decoration:underline">The App</span> is stored on a third party database service platform. Data we store on this service is subject to the services privacy policy and terms &amp; and conditions and any other future changes made to these or new policies or conditions.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">The App</span> will retain your Personal Data for as long as necessary to fulfill the purposes for which we collect it and as set out in this Privacy Notice and for the purpose of satisfying any legal, accounting, or reporting requirements that apply.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Rights of the Individual</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">a) Individuals whose data are processed by <span style="text-decoration:underline">The App</span> have the following rights related to protecting personal information:</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Right to Know: The individual has a right to obtain from us confirmation as to whether or not we are processing their Personal Data and, if so, the right to be provided with the information contained in this Privacy Notice.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Right to File Complaint: Individual may file a complaint with HorizonMind about concerns related to how data is being processed. If, for whatever reason, the individual feels we do not meet the standards expected of us, they are also entitled to make a complaint with a local supervisory authority (as applicable)</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Right to Access: Individuals have a right to access information about data being stored about them.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Right to Rectify: Individuals have the right to rectify inaccurate Personal Data and to have incomplete Personal Data completed.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Right to Restrict Use: Individuals have the right to place restrictions on our use of their Personal Data if they contest the accuracy of the Personal Data that we hold and we are verifying its accuracy; if we have used their Personal Data unlawfully (and they request restriction of its use rather than erasure); if we no longer need the Personal Data for the purpose(s) for which we collected it but they need it to deal with a legal claim; or they have objected to our use and we are analyzing whether our legitimate grounds override their right to object.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Right to Object: Individuals have the right to object to our use of their Personal Data where our reason for using it is based on our legitimate interest or their consent.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Right to Data Portability: Individuals have the right to have their Personal Data transferred in electronic copy to them or another party of their choosing. This right applies to Personal Data we are processing to service a contract with the individual and to Personal Data we are processing based on the individual’s consent. All requests to access data by an individual and is approved per legal requirements will be provided through a common data format. These formats will either be a comma-separated values file or a PDF document.</p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Right to be Forgotten: An individual may request that their personal data, contained within <span style="text-decoration:underline">The App</span> to be deleted. These “personal data deletion request” will be respected and actioned upon, regardless of circumstances, unless otherwise required by law. Should you want to delete your personal data then please request a deletion of your personal data as pertaining to your username by contacting the team here support@horizomind.io</p></li></ul><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">b) To exercise any of these rights, please contact us below.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Security</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We maintain commercially reasonable security measures to protect the Personal Data we collect and store from loss, misuse, destruction, or unauthorized access. However, no security measure or modality of data transmission over the Internet is 100% secure. Although we strive to use commercially acceptable means to protect your Personal Data, we cannot guarantee absolute security.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Children’s Privacy</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">The App</span> is not intended for children under 13 years of age. We do not knowingly collect, use, or disclose personal information from children under 13.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Notice to Nevada Residents</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Nevada law allows Nevada residents to opt-out of the sale of certain types of personal information. Subject to several exceptions, Nevada law defines “sale” to mean the exchange of certain types of personal information for monetary consideration to a person for the person to license or sell the information to additional persons. We do not currently sell personal information as defined in the Nevada law. However, if you are a Nevada resident, you still may submit a verified request to opt-out of sales and we will record your instructions and incorporate them in the future if our policy changes. Opt-out requests may be sent to support@horizomind.io</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Notice to California Residents</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">We do not disclose personal information obtained through our App to third parties for their direct marketing purposes. Accordingly, we have no obligations under California Civil Code § 1798.83.</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Contacting The Gift - Beta Team</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Email: support@horizomind.io</p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Updates to this Privacy Notice</strong></p><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">The App</span> and HorizonMind reserves the right to change this privacy notice as needed.
